#Dismantling Spanish Commonwealth
country_event = {

	id = 96043
	title = "EVTNAME96010" #The Treaty of $CAPITAL$
	desc = "EVTDESC96010"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	major = yes

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		war = no
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = great_war
			has_country_modifier = great_war2
			has_country_modifier = great_war3
			has_country_flag = in_great_war
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
		tag = SPC
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96010" #We welcome peace
		clr_country_flag = in_great_war
		clr_country_flag = calling_all_allies
		clr_country_flag = enemy_of_my_enemy
		clr_country_flag = total_collapse
		clr_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
		clr_country_flag = will_not_surrender
		clr_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		clr_country_flag = spc_commonwealth
		remove_country_modifier = great_war
		remove_country_modifier = great_war2
		remove_country_modifier = great_war3
		war_exhaustion = 40
		
        #### UNIQUE PART ####

		random_owned = {
		   limit = { owner = { capital = 487 } }
		   owner = { capital = 521 }
		}
		
		all_core = { remove_core = SPC }
		
		change_tag = SPA

        ##### UNIQUE PART ENDS HERE ####

		#if over the badboy limit, reduce infamy to 24.99, otherwise reduce infamy by 10
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { NOT = { badboy = 1 } }
			}
			owner = {
				badboy = -10
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { badboy = 1 }
			}
			owner = { badboy = -1000 }
			owner = { badboy = 24.99 }
		}

		#remove the ultimatum_refused global, if this is an Infamy war
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah } }
			owner = { clr_global_flag = ultimatum_refused }
		}

		#prestige hit
		prestige_factor = -0.5

		#remove cores on overseas provinces
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_overseas = yes
				is_core = THIS
			}
			remove_core = THIS
		}

		#normalize relations with treaty members
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			relation = { who = THIS value = 200 }
		}
		
		#release all cores to anyone with a truce
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				NOT = { this_culture_union = THIS }
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					is_core = THIS
					state_scope = {
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					}
				}
				remove_core = THIS
			}
			country_event = 96014
		}

		#release all vassals
		any_country = {
			limit = { vassal_of = THIS }
			leave_alliance = THIS
			country_event = 96015
		}			

		#release non-existing countries		
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					civilized = yes
					tag = JAP
					tag = KOR
					tag = SIA
					tag = MOR
					tag = ALD
					tag = TUN
					tag = EGY
				}
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no
				OR = {
					is_cultural_union = no
					tag = ROM
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_primary_culture = THIS
						culture_has_union_tag = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = { is_culture_group = iberian }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = post_colonial_country }
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					is_core = THIS
					state_scope = {
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					}
				}
				remove_core = THIS
			}
			country_event = 96012
		}

		any_country = {

				 }

						 }
					 }

			 }

				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 ai = yes
					 is_greater_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96016 days = 15 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 is_greater_power = no
					 is_secondary_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96017 days = 15 }
			 }
		 }

		#add fascism and punitive effects
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_ideology_enabled = fascist
					NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
					NOT = { government = fascist_monarchy }
				}
			}

						value = fascist
						factor = 0.2
					}
				}
				officers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }

						value = fascist
						factor = 0.4
					}
				}

						NOT = {
							OR = {
								type = soldiers
								type = officers
							}
						}
					}
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		#### UNIQUE PART ####

		}

			name = the_eye_of_the_storm
			duration = 365
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = punitive_effects
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = no_more_war
			duration = 3650
		}
	}

			add_country_modifier = { name = dismantling_country duration = 385 }
		}

		#Release organized colonies as vassals so other countries annex them later
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
				has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
			}
			country_event = 96095
		}
		
		#Release colonies as vassals so other countries annex them later
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
				capital_scope = {
					owned_by = THIS
					owner = { tech_school = developing_tech_school }
				}
			}
			country_event = 96095
		}

		 #give colonies without cores to truce GP's
		 random_owned = {
			 limit = {
				 OR = {
					 is_overseas = yes
					 is_colonial = yes
					 NOT = { is_core = TSS }
					 NOT = { is_core = YKT }
					 NOT = { is_core = THIS }
				 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 ai = no
					 is_greater_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96011 days = 10 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 ai = yes
					 is_greater_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96016 days = 15 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 is_greater_power = no
					 is_secondary_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96017 days = 15 }
			 }
		 }

		#add fascism and punitive effects
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_ideology_enabled = fascist
					NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
					NOT = { government = fascist_monarchy }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				soldiers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.2
					}
				}
				officers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.4
					}
				}
				any_pop = {
					limit = {
						is_primary_culture = yes
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								type = soldiers
								type = officers
							}
						}
					}
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = no_maelstrom_for_now
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = the_eye_of_the_storm
			duration = 365
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = punitive_effects
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = no_more_war
			duration = 3650
		}
		
		# Additions for Burgundy - This is where the regime implodes	
		# FRK has its own version
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { 
				    tag = BRG 
					OR = { 
					   ruling_party_ideology = paternal
					   ruling_party_ideology = fascist
					   ruling_party_ideology = communist
					}
			    }
			}
			owner = {
				plurality = 50
				nationalvalue = nv_liberty
				clr_country_flag = regime_collapse
	            set_country_flag = regime_collapse
				remove_country_modifier = regime_collapse
                remove_country_modifier = the_new_order_BRG				
		        add_country_modifier = {
                   name = regime_collapse
                   duration = 3650
                }
			}
		}	

		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { 
				    tag = PBG
					OR = { 
					   ruling_party_ideology = paternal
					   ruling_party_ideology = fascist
					   ruling_party_ideology = communist
					}
			    }
			}
			owner = {
				plurality = 50
				nationalvalue = nv_liberty
				clr_country_flag = regime_collapse
	            set_country_flag = regime_collapse
				remove_country_modifier = regime_collapse
                remove_country_modifier = the_new_order_BRG				
		        add_country_modifier = {
                   name = regime_collapse
                   duration = 3650
                }
			}
		}		
	}
}

#		}
#		
#		random_country = {
#			limit = {
#				NOT = { tag = THIS }
#				THIS = { any_owned_province = { is_core = GBU } }
#				has_country_flag = guine_bissau_master
#			}
#			country_event = 961000
#		}
#		
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = THIS }
				THIS = { any_owned_province = { is_core = ZIM } }
				has_country_flag = zimbabwe_master
			}
			country_event = 961000
		}
		
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = THIS }
				THIS = { any_owned_province = { is_core = MOZ } }
				has_country_flag = mozambique_master
			}
			country_event = 961000
		}

		#Set up modifiers for dismantlement
		add_country_modifier = { name = being_dismantled duration = 385 }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				truce_with = THIS
				has_recently_lost_war = no
				is_vassal = no
				any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
				OR = {
					is_secondary_power = yes
					is_greater_power = yes
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = dismantling_country duration = 385 }
		}

		#Release organized colonies as vassals so other countries annex them later
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
				has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
			}
			country_event = 96095
		}
		
		#Release colonies as vassals so other countries annex them later
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
				capital_scope = {
					owned_by = THIS
					owner = { tech_school = developing_tech_school }
				}
			}
			country_event = 96095
		}

		 #give colonies without cores to truce GP's
		 random_owned = {
			 limit = {
				 OR = {
					 is_overseas = yes
					 is_colonial = yes
					 NOT = { is_core = TSS }
					 NOT = { is_core = YKT }
					 NOT = { is_core = THIS }
				 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 ai = no
					 is_greater_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96011 days = 10 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 ai = yes
					 is_greater_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96016 days = 15 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 is_greater_power = no
					 is_secondary_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96017 days = 15 }
			 }
		 }

		#add fascism and punitive effects
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_ideology_enabled = fascist
					NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
					NOT = { government = fascist_monarchy }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				soldiers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.2
					}
				}
				officers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.4
					}
				}
				any_pop = {
					limit = {
						is_primary_culture = yes
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								type = soldiers
								type = officers
							}
						}
					}
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = no_maelstrom_for_now
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = the_eye_of_the_storm
			duration = 365
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = punitive_effects
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = no_more_war
			duration = 3650
		}		
	}
}

#### Dismantling Russia ( This is the non-total dismantlement ) #####

country_event = {

	id = 96046
	title = "EVTNAME96010" #The Treaty of $CAPITAL$
	desc = "EVTDESC96010"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	major = yes

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		war = no
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = great_war
			has_country_modifier = great_war2
			has_country_modifier = great_war3
			has_country_flag = in_great_war
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
		tag = RUS
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_dismantled_once }
		NOT = { truce_with = TAR }
		NOT = { truce_with = PLC }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96010" #We welcome peace
		clr_country_flag = in_great_war
		clr_country_flag = calling_all_allies
		clr_country_flag = enemy_of_my_enemy
		clr_country_flag = total_collapse
		clr_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
		clr_country_flag = will_not_surrender
		clr_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		remove_country_modifier = great_war
		remove_country_modifier = great_war2
		remove_country_modifier = great_war3
		war_exhaustion = 40
		
        #### UNIQUE PART ####
		
	    set_country_flag = RUS_dismantled_once

        ##### UNIQUE PART ENDS HERE ####

		#if over the badboy limit, reduce infamy to 24.99, otherwise reduce infamy by 10
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { NOT = { badboy = 1 } }
			}
			owner = {
				badboy = -10
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { badboy = 1 }
			}
			owner = { badboy = -1000 }
			owner = { badboy = 24.99 }
		}

		#remove the ultimatum_refused global, if this is an Infamy war
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah } }
			owner = { clr_global_flag = ultimatum_refused }
		}

		#prestige hit
		prestige_factor = -0.5

		#remove cores on overseas provinces
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_overseas = yes
				is_core = THIS
			}
			remove_core = THIS
		}

		#normalize relations with treaty members
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			relation = { who = THIS value = 200 }
		}
		
		#release all cores to anyone with a truce
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				NOT = { this_culture_union = THIS }
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					is_core = THIS
					state_scope = {
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					}
				}
				remove_core = THIS
			}
			country_event = 96014
		}

		#release all vassals
		any_country = {
			limit = { vassal_of = THIS }
			leave_alliance = THIS
			country_event = 96015
		}			
		
		#release non-existing countries	( Tatars and Ural tags are excluded from this script )		
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					civilized = yes
					tag = JAP
					tag = KOR
					tag = SIA
					tag = MOR
					tag = ALD
					tag = TUN
					tag = EGY
				}
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no
				OR = {
					is_cultural_union = no
					tag = ROM
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_primary_culture = THIS
						culture_has_union_tag = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = { is_culture_group = east_slavic }
				NOT = { is_culture_group = uralic }
				NOT = { is_primary_culture = tatar }
				NOT = { is_primary_culture = bashkir }
				NOT = { tag = KAZ }
				NOT = { tag = BAH }
				NOT = { tag = KHK }
				NOT = { tag = MOS }
				NOT = { tag = NOV }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = post_colonial_country }
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					is_core = THIS
					state_scope = {
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					}
				}
				remove_core = THIS

			country_event = 96012
		}

					 is_secondary_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96017 days = 15 }
			 }
		 }

		#add fascism and punitive effects
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_ideology_enabled = fascist
					NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
					NOT = { government = fascist_monarchy }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				soldiers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.2
					}
				}
				officers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.4
					}
				}
				any_pop = {
					limit = {
						is_primary_culture = yes
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								type = soldiers
								type = officers
							}
						}
					}
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = no_maelstrom_for_now
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = the_eye_of_the_storm
			duration = 365
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = punitive_effects
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = no_more_war
			duration = 3650
		}
		
		#### Ensure cores are added back to particular critical states which should not have cores removed ###
		
		RUS_946 = { add_core = RUS }
        RUS_962 = { add_core = RUS }	

        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = russian_karelia } } owner = { clr_country_flag = russian_karelia } }		
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = the_cossack_claims } } owner = { clr_country_flag = the_cossack_claims } }	
		
		### Ensure cores are added back to particular critical states which should not have cores removed ###
		
	}
}

#### Dismantling Russia (Total Dismantlement) #####

country_event = {

	id = 96047
	title = "EVTNAME96010" #The Treaty of $CAPITAL$
	desc = "EVTDESC96010"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	major = yes

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		war = no
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = great_war
			has_country_modifier = great_war2
			has_country_modifier = great_war3
			has_country_flag = in_great_war

        }
	}

		days = 10
	}

        NOV = { clr_country_flag = unreleasable_country }

	option = {

		clr_country_flag = enemy_of_my_enemy

		clr_country_flag = will_not_surrender
		clr_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		remove_country_modifier = great_war
		remove_country_modifier = great_war2
		remove_country_modifier = great_war3
		war_exhaustion = 40	
		
		#if over the badboy limit, reduce infamy to 24.99, otherwise reduce infamy by 10
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { NOT = { badboy = 1 } }
			}
			owner = {
				badboy = -10
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { badboy = 1 }
			}
			owner = { badboy = -1000 }
			owner = { badboy = 24.99 }
		}

		#remove the ultimatum_refused global, if this is an Infamy war

			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah } }
			owner = { clr_global_flag = ultimatum_refused }
		}

		#prestige hit
		prestige_factor = -0.9

		#remove cores on overseas provinces
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_overseas = yes
				is_core = THIS

			remove_core = THIS

						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			relation = { who = THIS value = 200 }
		}

					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}

					is_core = THIS

						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }

				remove_core = THIS

				is_core = THIS
			}

		}

		#normalize relations with treaty members
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			relation = { who = THIS value = 200 }
		}
		
		#release all cores to anyone with a truce
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }

				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					is_core = THIS
					state_scope = {
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					}
				}
				remove_core = THIS
			}
			country_event = 96014
		}

		#release all vassals
		any_country = {
			limit = { vassal_of = THIS }
			leave_alliance = THIS
			country_event = 96015
		}		

		#release non-existing countries			
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					civilized = yes
					tag = JAP
					tag = KOR
					tag = SIA
					tag = MOR

					is_cultural_union = no
					tag = ROM
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_primary_culture = THIS
						culture_has_union_tag = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = { primary_culture = septiman }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = post_colonial_country }
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					is_core = THIS
					state_scope = {
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					}
				}
				remove_core = THIS
			}
			country_event = 96012
		}
		
        #if Plantagenia or has a truce, then give back the most important state
        random_country = {
            limit = {
                tag = PLA
                truce_with = THIS
                THIS = {
                    NOT = {
                        any_owned_province = {
                           region = PLA_214
                        }
                    }
                }
                THIS = { owns = 205 }
            }
            PLA_214 = { add_core = PLA }		
            THIS = {
                any_owned = {
                    limit = { is_core = PLA }
                    secede_province = PLA
                }
            }
        }
		
        #if Plantagenia has a truce, and the CBV is not owned, annex CBV and set flag
        random_country = {
            limit = {
                tag = PLA
                truce_with = THIS
                THIS = {
                    NOT = {

                           region = NBG_220

                }
            }
        }
		
		#give cores back to neighboring, non-allied countries
		any_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				NOT = { alliance_with = THIS }
				NOT = { truce_with = THIS }
				NOT = { this_culture_union = THIS }
			}

							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96011 days = 10 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 ai = yes
					 is_greater_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96016 days = 15 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 is_greater_power = no
					 is_secondary_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96017 days = 15 }
			 }
		 }

		#add fascism and punitive effects
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_ideology_enabled = fascist
					NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
					NOT = { government = fascist_monarchy }
				}
			}

						value = fascist
						factor = 0.2
					}
				}
				officers = {

					ideology = {

						factor = 0.4
					}

							OR = {
								type = soldiers
								type = officers
							}
						}
					}
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = no_maelstrom_for_now

			name = the_eye_of_the_storm

			duration = 1825
		}

			name = no_more_war
			duration = 3650
		}
	}

#####Dismantlement of Bohemian Tags (such as BOH or HLR or GCF or HRE
country_event = {

	id = 96050
	title = "EVTNAME96010" #The Treaty of $CAPITAL$
	desc = "EVTDESC96010"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	major = yes

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		war = no
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = great_war
			has_country_modifier = great_war2
			has_country_modifier = great_war3
			has_country_flag = in_great_war
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
		OR = {
		  tag = BOH
		  tag = HLR
		  tag = GCF
		  tag = CAE
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96010" #We welcome peace
		clr_country_flag = dismantle_declared
		clr_country_flag = in_great_war
		clr_country_flag = calling_all_allies
		clr_country_flag = enemy_of_my_enemy
		clr_country_flag = total_collapse
		clr_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
		clr_country_flag = will_not_surrender
		clr_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
        remove_country_modifier = ready_for_rot
		remove_country_modifier = great_war
		remove_country_modifier = great_war2
		remove_country_modifier = great_war3
		war_exhaustion = 40
		
		# Remove Primary Cores for Non-BOH
		
		random_owned = {
		    limit = {
		       owner = { tag = HLR }
			}
		    owner = { all_core = { remove_core = HLR } }
		}

		random_owned = {
		    limit = {
		       owner = { tag = GCF }
			}
		    owner = { all_core = { remove_core = GCF } }
		}

		random_owned = {
		    limit = {
		       owner = { tag = CAE }
			}
		    owner = { all_core = { remove_core = CAE } }
		}
		
		# Make sure that this tag does not have cores on Germany
		
		GER = { all_core = { remove_core = THIS } }
		
		# Istria will be liberated
		
		AUS_736 = { remove_core = THIS }
		
		# Add Swabian and Confederation Cores to allow for Dismantlement
		
        566 = { add_core = CFR }
	    564 = { add_core = CFR }
	    540 = { add_core = CFR }
        MNR_581 = { add_core = CFR }
        MNR_585 = { add_core = CFR }	
        HSK_583 = { add_core = CFR }	
        PRU_575 = { add_core = CFR }
        HES_564 = { add_core = CFR }
		
		589 = { add_core = SWA }
		590 = { add_core = SWA }
		591 = { add_core = SWA }
		594 = { add_core = SWA }
		593 = { add_core = SWA }			
		BAD_586 = { add_core = SWA }
		SWI_603 = { add_core = SWA }
	    SWI_605 = { add_core = SWA }
		
		# Add Back Bohemian Cores as a Failsafe
		
		BOH_629 = { add_core = BOH }
		AUS_625 = { add_core = BOH }
		AUS_626 = { add_core = BOH }
		PRU_682 = { add_core = BOH }
		
		# Add Teschen Cores to Lower Silesia
		
		SIL_684 = { add_core = TES }
		
		# Release FRE if it is a vassal
		
        random_country = {
            limit = {
                tag = FRE
                vassal_of = THIS
            }
            THIS = {
                release_vassal = FRE
            }
        }		
		
        #If any burgundian tag has a truce then give them Swabia and Confederation as puppets
		
        random_country = {
            limit = {
                tag = PBG
                truce_with = THIS
				# Frankfurt
                THIS = { owns = 564 }
            }
            THIS = {
                any_owned = {
                    limit = { is_core = CFR }
                    secede_province = PBG
                }
            }
            release_vassal = CFR
            diplomatic_influence = {
                who = CFR
                value = 200

		change_tag = BOH
	}

#####Dismantlement of German Subtags
country_event = {

	id = 96051
	title = "EVTNAME96010" #The Treaty of $CAPITAL$
	desc = "EVTDESC96010"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	major = yes

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		war = no
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = great_war
			has_country_modifier = great_war2
			has_country_modifier = great_war3
			has_country_flag = in_great_war
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
		OR = {
		  tag = SGF
		  tag = NGF
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96010" #We welcome peace
		clr_country_flag = dismantle_declared
		clr_country_flag = in_great_war
		clr_country_flag = calling_all_allies
		clr_country_flag = enemy_of_my_enemy
		clr_country_flag = total_collapse
		clr_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
		clr_country_flag = will_not_surrender
		clr_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		remove_country_modifier = ready_for_rot
		remove_country_modifier = great_war
		remove_country_modifier = great_war2

						 }

					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no

					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96016 days = 15 }
			 }
			 any_country = {

					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 is_greater_power = no
					 is_secondary_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96017 days = 15 }
			 }
		 }

		#add fascism and punitive effects
		random_owned = {

					NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
					NOT = { government = fascist_monarchy }

						factor = 0.2
					}
				}

						factor = 0.4
					}

							OR = {
								type = soldiers
								type = officers
							}
						}
					}

						value = fascist
						factor = 0.1
					}
				}
			}
		}

			name = the_eye_of_the_storm
			duration = 365
		}

			name = punitive_effects
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = no_more_war
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
}

#####Dismantlement of Big Boy Germany
country_event = {

	id = 96052
	title = "EVTNAME96010" #The Treaty of $CAPITAL$
	desc = "EVTDESC96010"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	major = yes

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		war = no
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = great_war
			has_country_modifier = great_war2
			has_country_modifier = great_war3
			has_country_flag = in_great_war
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
		tag = GER
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96010" #We welcome peace
		set_country_flag = GERMANY_LOST
		clr_country_flag = dismantle_declared
		clr_country_flag = in_great_war
		clr_country_flag = calling_all_allies
		clr_country_flag = enemy_of_my_enemy
		clr_country_flag = total_collapse

		}
	}

		days = 10
	}

				badboy = -10
			}

			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah } }
			owner = { clr_global_flag = ultimatum_refused }
		}

		#prestige hit
		prestige_factor = -0.5

		#remove cores on overseas provinces
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_overseas = yes
				is_core = THIS
			}
			remove_core = THIS
		}

		#normalize relations with treaty members
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			relation = { who = THIS value = 200 }
		}
		
		#release all cores to anyone with a truce
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				NOT = { this_culture_union = THIS }
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					is_core = THIS
					state_scope = {
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					}
				}
				remove_core = THIS
			}
			country_event = 96014
		}

		#release all vassals
		any_country = {
			limit = { vassal_of = THIS }
			leave_alliance = THIS
			country_event = 96015
		}		

		#release non-existing countries			
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					civilized = yes
					tag = JAP
					tag = KOR
					tag = SIA
					tag = MOR
					tag = ALD

				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no

					is_cultural_union = no
					tag = ROM
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_primary_culture = THIS
						culture_has_union_tag = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = { primary_culture = north_italian }
				NOT = { primary_culture = central_italian }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = post_colonial_country }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = unreleasable_country }
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					is_core = THIS
					state_scope = {
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					}
				}
				remove_core = THIS
			}
			country_event = 96012
		}

		#give cores back to neighboring, non-allied countries
		any_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				NOT = { alliance_with = THIS }
				NOT = { truce_with = THIS }
				NOT = { this_culture_union = THIS }
			}
			country_event = 96013
		}

		#Give up partial colonies to proper colonial masters

					 ai = no

					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }

						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96011 days = 10 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 ai = yes
					 is_greater_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96016 days = 15 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 is_greater_power = no
					 is_secondary_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96017 days = 15 }
			 }
		 }

		#add fascism and punitive effects
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_ideology_enabled = fascist
					NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
					NOT = { government = fascist_monarchy }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				soldiers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.2
					}
				}
				officers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.4
					}
				}
				any_pop = {
					limit = {
						is_primary_culture = yes
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								type = soldiers
								type = officers
							}
						}
					}
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = no_maelstrom_for_now
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = the_eye_of_the_storm
			duration = 365
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = punitive_effects
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = no_more_war
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
}

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		war = no

		days = 10
	}

		any_neighbor_country = {

						 }

			 }

				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 ai = yes
					 is_greater_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96016 days = 15 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 is_greater_power = no
					 is_secondary_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96017 days = 15 }
			 }
		 }

		#add fascism and punitive effects
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_ideology_enabled = fascist
					NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
					NOT = { government = fascist_monarchy }
				}
			}
			owner = {

						value = fascist
						factor = 0.2
					}
				}
				officers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.4
					}
				}

					limit = {
						is_primary_culture = yes
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								type = soldiers
								type = officers
							}
						}
					}
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = no_maelstrom_for_now

			name = the_eye_of_the_storm
			duration = 365
		}

			name = punitive_effects
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = no_more_war
			duration = 3650
		}			
	}
}

#### Dismantling Japan

#### This is a relatively generic script unless specific conditions are met

country_event = {

	id = 96055
	title = "EVTNAME96010" #The Treaty of $CAPITAL$
	desc = "EVTDESC96010"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC96010_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	major = yes

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		war = no
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = great_war
			has_country_modifier = great_war2
			has_country_modifier = great_war3
			has_country_flag = in_great_war
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
		tag = JAP
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
			has_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96010" #We welcome peace
		
		clr_country_flag = dismantle_declared
		clr_country_flag = in_great_war
		clr_country_flag = calling_all_allies
		clr_country_flag = enemy_of_my_enemy
		clr_country_flag = total_collapse
		clr_country_flag = ultimatum_accepted
		clr_country_flag = will_not_surrender
		clr_country_flag = dismantling_treaty
		remove_country_modifier = great_war
		remove_country_modifier = great_war2
		remove_country_modifier = great_war3
		war_exhaustion = 40
		
        #### UNIQUE PART ####
		
		#### Remove Japanese Cores on Questionable Territories ###
		
        1678 = { remove_core = JAP add_core = RYU }
		1679 = { remove_core = JAP add_core = RYU }
		
		any_owned = { 
		   limit = {
		      OR = {
		         is_core = KOR 
			     is_core = GOY
		      }
		   }
		   remove_core = JAP 
		}
		
		any_owned = { 
		   limit = {
		      is_core = TAW
		   }
		   remove_core = JAP 
		}
		
		#### Trigger the End of Japan Event Chain in one day. Set the Transitional Government Flag. ###
		
		random_owned = {
		    limit = {
		       owner = { has_country_flag = japan_compromised }
            }
            owner = { 
			   country_event = { id = 164125 days = 1 } 
	           government = hms_government
	           political_reform = state_equal_weight
	           political_reform = universal_weighted_voting
 	           political_reform = yes_meeting
	           political_reform = censored_press
	           political_reform = no_trade_unions
	           political_reform = first_past_the_post
	           political_reform = non_secret_ballots
			   set_country_flag = transitional_government
			}			
		}		
		
		### Inherit Kamchatka if it exists
		
		any_country = {
            limit = {
               tag = KAM 
               vassal_of = THIS 
            }
            annex_to = JAP 
        }			
		
		### Force-Release Ryukyu due to it being Primary Japanese
		
		any_owned = { 
		   limit = {
		      is_core = RYU
		   }
		   secede_province = RYU
		}
				
		### China always gets first dibs on the Siberian Cores if it holds any ###
		
        random_country = {
            limit = {
			    tag = CHI
				exists = yes
                truce_with = THIS
            }
            THIS = {
                any_owned = {
                    limit = { is_core = CHI }
					remove_core = THIS
                    secede_province = CHI
                }
            }
        }
		
        random_country = {
            limit = {
			    tag = KMT
				exists = yes
                truce_with = THIS
            }
            THIS = {
                any_owned = {
                    limit = { is_core = KMT }
					remove_core = THIS
                    secede_province = KMT
                }
            }
        }
		
		### Russia gets second dibs on the Siberian Cores ###
		
        random_country = {
            limit = {
			    tag = RUS
				exists = yes
                truce_with = THIS
            }
            THIS = {
                any_owned = {
                    limit = { is_core = RUS }
					remove_core = THIS
                    secede_province = RUS
                }
            }
        }
		
		#if over the badboy limit, reduce infamy to 24.99, otherwise reduce infamy by 10
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { NOT = { badboy = 1 } }
			}
			owner = {
				badboy = -10
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { badboy = 1 }
			}
			owner = { badboy = -1000 }
			owner = { badboy = 24.99 }
		}

		#remove the ultimatum_refused global, if this is an Infamy war
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah } }
			owner = { clr_global_flag = ultimatum_refused }
		}

		#prestige hit
		prestige_factor = -0.5

		#remove cores on overseas provinces
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_overseas = yes
				is_core = THIS
			}
			remove_core = THIS
		}

		#normalize relations with treaty members
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			relation = { who = THIS value = 200 }
		}
		
		#release all cores to anyone with a truce
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				NOT = { this_culture_union = THIS }
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					is_core = THIS
					state_scope = {
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					}
				}
				remove_core = THIS
			}
			country_event = 96014
		}

		#release all vassals
		any_country = {
			limit = { vassal_of = THIS }
			leave_alliance = THIS
			country_event = 96015
		}		

		#release non-existing countries			
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					civilized = yes
					tag = JAP
					tag = KOR
					tag = SIA
					tag = MOR
					tag = ALD
					tag = TUN
					tag = EGY
				}
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no
				OR = {
					is_cultural_union = no
					tag = ROM
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_primary_culture = THIS
						culture_has_union_tag = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = { primary_culture = japanese }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = post_colonial_country }
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					is_core = THIS
					state_scope = {
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					}
				}
				remove_core = THIS
			}
			country_event = 96012
		}

		#give cores back to neighboring, non-allied countries
		any_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				NOT = { alliance_with = THIS }
				NOT = { truce_with = THIS }
				NOT = { this_culture_union = THIS }
			}
			country_event = 96013
		}

		#################Colonial Dismantlement#################
		#Give up partial colonies to proper colonial masters
		
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = THIS }
				THIS = { any_owned_province = { is_core = NGR } }
				has_country_flag = nigeria_master
			}
			country_event = 961000
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = THIS }
				THIS = { any_owned_province = { is_core = CHR } }
				has_country_flag = christiania_master
			}
			country_event = 961000
		}

			}
			country_event = 961000

			}
			country_event = 961000
		}

		#Set up modifiers for dismantlement
		add_country_modifier = { name = being_dismantled duration = 385 }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				truce_with = THIS
				has_recently_lost_war = no
				is_vassal = no
				any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
				OR = {
					is_secondary_power = yes
					is_greater_power = yes
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = dismantling_country duration = 385 }
		}

		#Release organized colonies as vassals so other countries annex them later
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
				has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
			}
			country_event = 96095
		}
		
		#Release colonies as vassals so other countries annex them later
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
				capital_scope = {
					owned_by = THIS
					owner = { tech_school = developing_tech_school }
				}
			}
			country_event = 96095
		}

		 #give colonies without cores to truce GP's
		 random_owned = {
			 limit = {
				 OR = {
					 is_overseas = yes
					 is_colonial = yes
					 NOT = { is_core = TSS }
					 NOT = { is_core = YKT }
					 NOT = { is_core = THIS }
				 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 ai = no
					 is_greater_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96011 days = 10 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 ai = yes
					 is_greater_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96016 days = 15 }
			 }
			 any_country = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = {
						 any_greater_power = {
							 ai = no
							 truce_with = THIS
						 }
					 }
					 is_greater_power = no
					 is_secondary_power = yes
					 exists = yes
					 has_recently_lost_war = no
					 is_vassal = no
					 any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
					 OR = {
						 truce_with = THIS
						 AND = {
							 THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							 has_country_flag = coalition_member
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 country_event = { id = 96017 days = 15 }
			 }
		 }

		#add fascism and punitive effects
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_ideology_enabled = fascist
					NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
					NOT = { government = fascist_monarchy }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				soldiers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.2
					}
				}
				officers = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.4
					}
				}
				any_pop = {
					limit = {
						is_primary_culture = yes
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								type = soldiers
								type = officers
							}
						}
					}
					ideology = {
						value = fascist
						factor = 0.1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = no_maelstrom_for_now
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = the_eye_of_the_storm
			duration = 365
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = punitive_effects
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = no_more_war
			duration = 3650
		}			
	}
}

#################################################
#												#
#     	Events that Start a Great War			#
#												#
#################################################

country_event = {

	id = 96065
	title = "EVTNAME96065" #Outrage!
	desc = "EVTDESC96065"
	picture = "Demonstration"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		war = no
		is_greater_power = yes
		is_disarmed = no
		mass_politics = 1
		any_greater_power = {
			is_disarmed = no
			NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -100 } }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality }
			NOT = { tag = THIS }
			NOT = { truce_with = THIS }
		}		
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = no_more_war
			has_country_modifier = neutrality
			war_policy = pacifism
			any_greater_power = { has_country_flag = in_great_war }
			AND = {
			   OR = {
			      tag = GCF
				  tag = SGF
				  tag = NGF
			   }
			   NOT = { has_country_flag = phoenix_rot }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			war_policy = jingoism
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				government = absolute_monarchy
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				government = fascist_monarchy
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				government = democracy
				government = parliamentary_republic 
				government = hms_government
				government = socialist_republic
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			war_policy = anti_military
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_greater_power = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96065" #We must defend $COUNTRY_ADJ$ interests, no matter the cost.
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				is_disarmed = no
				NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -100 } }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality }
			}
			add_casus_belli = {
				target = THIS
				type = dismantle_cb
				months = 12
			}
		}
		any_pop = {
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.02
				value = jingoism
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = pacifism
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				war_policy = anti_military
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				num_of_revolts = 1
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				num_of_revolts = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				NOT = { total_amount_of_divisions = 10 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB96065" #We cannot afford such a war.
		prestige_factor = -0.1
		any_pop = {
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.02
				value = pacifism
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = jingoism
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				war_policy = jingoism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				war_policy = anti_military
			}
		}
	}
}

#########################################################
#														#
#      		Transfer of the Colonies					#
#														#
#########################################################

#Transfer all colonies which are coastal and NOT currently bordering a truce country
country_event = {

	id = 96070
	title = "EVTNAME96070" #The $COUNTRY_ADJ$ Colonies
	desc = "EVTDESC96070"
	picture = "treaty"

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		war = no
		has_country_modifier = punitive_effects
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				is_colonial = yes
				is_overseas = yes
			}
			port = yes
			NOT = { is_core = THIS }
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							is_greater_power = yes
							is_secondary_power = yes
						}
						OR = {
							truce_with = THIS
							AND = {
								THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
								has_country_flag = coalition_member
							}
						}
						NOT = { has_country_flag = not_want_colonies }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		any_greater_power = {
			OR = {
				truce_with = THIS
				AND = {
					THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
					has_country_flag = coalition_member
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = not_want_colonies }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96070" #Time to carve up our empire.
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_greater_power = yes
					is_secondary_power = yes
				}
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = not_want_colonies }
			}
			country_event = 96071
		}
	}
}

				OR = {

					is_overseas = yes
				}
				port = yes
				NOT = { is_core = THIS }
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								is_greater_power = yes
								is_secondary_power = yes
							}
							OR = {
								truce_with = THIS
								AND = {
									THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
									has_country_flag = coalition_member
								}
							}
							NOT = { has_country_flag = not_want_colonies }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				is_colonial = yes
				is_overseas = yes
			}
			NOT = { is_core = THIS }
			any_neighbor_province = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						is_greater_power = yes
						is_secondary_power = yes
					}
					OR = {
						truce_with = THIS
						AND = {
							THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
							has_country_flag = coalition_member
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = not_want_colonies }
				}
			}
		}
		any_greater_power = {
			OR = {
				truce_with = THIS
				AND = {
					THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
					has_country_flag = coalition_member
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = not_want_colonies }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96070" #Time to carve up our empire.
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_greater_power = yes
					is_secondary_power = yes
				}
				OR = {
					truce_with = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = not_want_colonies }
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owned_by = THIS
						OR = {
							is_colonial = yes
							is_overseas = yes
						}
						NOT = { is_core = THIS }
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = 96076
		}
	}
}

				has_country_flag = friendly_democracy

#The Fate of $COUNTRY$ Colony
country_event = {
	id = 96095
	title = "EVTNAME96095" 
	desc = "EVTDESC96095"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			any_owned = {
				limit = { is_core = THIS }
				secede_province = THIS
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVT96095OPTA"
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = colony_to_be_annexed_flag } } }
			owner = { set_country_flag = colony_to_be_annexed_flag }
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = colony_to_be_annexed } } }
			owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = colony_to_be_annexed duration = 385 } }
		}
		
		# random_owned = {
			# limit = { is_core = FROM }
			# owner = { all_core = { remove_core = FROM } }
		# }
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { is_vassal = no } }
			owner = { FROM = { create_vassal = THIS } }
		}
		
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 30 } }
			10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 40 } }
			10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 50 } }
			10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 60 } }
			10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 70 } }
			10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 80 } }
			10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 90 } }
			10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 100 } }
			10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 110 } }
			10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 120 } }
		}
		
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_vassal = no
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = considering_colonial_offer }
				THIS = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = being_dismantled } }
				OR = {
					neighbour = THIS
					AND = {
						THIS = { num_of_ports = 1 }
						num_of_ports = 1
					}
				}
				OR = {
					is_greater_power = yes
					is_secondary_power = yes
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						truce_with = FROM
						has_country_modifier = dismantling_country
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = international_pariah } }
						has_country_flag = coalition_member
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = considering_colonial_offer duration = 2 }
			random_list = {
				25 = { country_event = 96096 }
				25 = { country_event = { id = 96096 days = 1 } }
				25 = { country_event = { id = 96096 days = 2 } }
				25 = { country_event = { id = 96096 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC96097"
	picture = "treaty"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		remove_country_modifier = colony_to_be_annexed
		clr_country_flag = colony_to_be_annexed_flag
		neutrality = yes
		overlord = {
			release_vassal = THIS
			leave_alliance = THIS
			relation = { who = THIS value = -300 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96097" #We submit
		civilized = no
		annex_to = FROM
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
            OR = {
		        tag = BEN
		        tag = PRF
				tag = PAK
				tag = MUG
				tag = RAJ
				tag = TRA
		        }		
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB96097" #We will never give up
		FROM = { country_event = 96099 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { total_pops = 2500000 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				total_pops = 3000000
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				total_pops = 3500000
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				total_pops = 4000000
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				total_pops = 4500000
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				total_pops = 5000000
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
				tag = HND
		        tag = BEN
		        tag = PRF
				tag = PAK
				tag = MUG
				tag = RAJ
				tag = TRA
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				capital_scope = { continent = africa }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Nation gets informed that colony refuses to submit
country_event = {
	
	id = 96099
	title = "EVTNAME96099"
	desc = "EVTDESC96099"
	picture = "treaty"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA96099" #War it is!
		badboy = 1
		casus_belli = {
			target = FROM
			type = conquest_any
			months = 12
		}
		war = {
			target = FROM
			attacker_goal = { casus_belli = conquest_any }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				badboy = 0.97
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB96099" #Let it go
		badboy = -1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { military_score = FROM } }
			modifier = { factor = 1.5 NOT = { FROM = { brigades_compare = 1.5 } } }
		}
	}
}
